  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_d7997b66-7c1a-4bd1-a42e-2a235f609210'
      });

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer9313499679023098085">Anna-Simone is a savvy television producer, desperate to find her place in lifestyle television. The colour, the madness and the manic deadlines form the perfect harmony of creative chaos she knows she can tackle. Enter Sky-High, the top-rated television network in the country, taking a chance on the ‘yes’ girl of the century. In a gut-wrenching twist of events, the talent</span>
  <span id="freeText9313499679023098085" style="display:none">Anna-Simone is a savvy television producer, desperate to find her place in lifestyle television. The colour, the madness and the manic deadlines form the perfect harmony of creative chaos she knows she can tackle. Enter Sky-High, the top-rated television network in the country, taking a chance on the ‘yes’ girl of the century. In a gut-wrenching twist of events, the talented producer meets Satan in stilettoes: a hellish nightmare of a woman who goes by the name Klarissa Maree-Francis. Well-heeled, well-spoken and a subscriber to the mean-girls group in media, Klarissa will make Anna-Simone question her very existence. From Louboutin cliques to live crosses gone wrong, Klarissa is set on making each day difficult for her team of fifteen producers – namely Anna-Simone. One by one her team will leave the battalion, shot down too many times, their brilliant ideas lying dead on the cutting room floor. See what happens when two alpha females go head to head. When women sell their souls for a promotion. Where the price of success costs you your sanity. Where the ultimate lows lead to creative highs and where out of the darkness, unlikely heroes emerge.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9313499679023098085" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2203647932" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2203647932" />
    <a title="8th Day Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74583594-8th-day-reads"><img alt="8th Day Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1512397836p2/74583594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2203647932?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="8th Day Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="8th Day Reads" href="/user/show/74583594-8th-day-reads">8th Day Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2203647932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13376975146670810560">If you have ever rooted for the underdog, or been the underdog yourself, Louboutins, Lattes, and Live TV by Miriam Sawan is the book for you. Along the same lines as The Devil Wears Prada, the story follows a youngish Anna-Simone, a vibrant television producer. She is already successful and takes on a new project, the tv show, Sky High. When she meets the infamous Klarissa Maree-Francis, she knows she has met her match and her nemesis. This story is written with a lot of punch, and seriously mak</span>
  <span id="freeText13376975146670810560" style="display:none">If you have ever rooted for the underdog, or been the underdog yourself, Louboutins, Lattes, and Live TV by Miriam Sawan is the book for you. Along the same lines as The Devil Wears Prada, the story follows a youngish Anna-Simone, a vibrant television producer. She is already successful and takes on a new project, the tv show, Sky High. When she meets the infamous Klarissa Maree-Francis, she knows she has met her match and her nemesis. This story is written with a lot of punch, and seriously make you concerned about the mental health of your coworkers. Klarissa will do just about anything to undermine the success of Miriam. It is a fast paced read for sure, full of great moments, some that make you laugh, some that make you shake your head in disbelief. A bit of a salacious read, this novel takes on the bully and ultimately the good and successful person wins in the end. Highly recommend for a light, fun, reading diversion with just enough sass and entertainment factors to keep most readers engaged until the end.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13376975146670810560" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17135412346115726085">Anna-Simone has started a dream new job at a top TV station, but unfortunately it comes with Klarissa, who would be best described as an epic b****. She seems to take delight in putting down all those that work around her, and seems to keep her cruelest scheming for Anna-Simone. As a result Anna-Simone really starts to doubt herself and her abilities.   <span id="freeText17135412346115726085" style="display:none">Anna-Simone has started a dream new job at a top TV station, but unfortunately it comes with Klarissa, who would be best described as an epic b****. She seems to take delight in putting down all those that work around her, and seems to keep her cruelest scheming for Anna-Simone. As a result Anna-Simone really starts to doubt herself and her abilities. Will she find the strength to stand up to her tormentor.<br /><br />This entertaining, funny and gasp-inducing novel, also has a really important message. There is a real strong anti-bullying theme that is ingrained in the plot. It does give a feeling of empowerment, in that you can and should stand up for yourself if you are being treated unfairly, and you can succeed, no matter how hard the Klarissa in your life, tries to convince you otherwise.<br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer160353184933945259">This is the perfect novel for fans of the like of The Devil Wears Prada, or for anyone who has had an absolute nightmare of a co-worker, who would throw you under bus at the blink of an eye. Many of us have been in a similar situation that protagonist, Anna-Simone finds herself in – battling a workplace foe, that seems to want to destroy her for no reason at all. It is shocking the lengths that Klarissa will go to, to undermine and humiliate her co-workers, just to get ahead. Her willingness to </span>
  <span id="freeText160353184933945259" style="display:none">This is the perfect novel for fans of the like of The Devil Wears Prada, or for anyone who has had an absolute nightmare of a co-worker, who would throw you under bus at the blink of an eye. Many of us have been in a similar situation that protagonist, Anna-Simone finds herself in – battling a workplace foe, that seems to want to destroy her for no reason at all. It is shocking the lengths that Klarissa will go to, to undermine and humiliate her co-workers, just to get ahead. Her willingness to betray and bully, makes for a compelling read...it certainly kept me turning page after page, hoping the next one will bring her comeuppance. I don't want to give away any spoilers, but you wont be disappointed by the ending, so fight through your frustrations. Louboutins, Lattes &amp; Live TV by Miriam Sawan is a really fun read, that had be laughing out loud, wanting to tear my hair out, and definitely will make me think twice before sending that brusque email. </span>

<div id="review_2212234277" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2212234277" />
    <a title="Library Love" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74893905-library-love"><img alt="Library Love" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513106838p2/74893905.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2212234277?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Library Love" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Library Love" href="/user/show/74893905-library-love">Library Love</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2212234277" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8107618369193446473">'Louboutins, Lattes & Live TV' by Miriam Sawan, is the epitome of guilty pleasure reading. There is plenty of back-stabbing, heaps of drama, and a bucket load of salacious gossip. This talented author has created a novel that is so well-written, and so readable that I finished it in a single day. T is such a page turner - I just had to know what would happen next<br/><br/>The story follows Anna-Simone, delighted to land a job at Sky High, a prestigious television network. However, it doesn't take long for</span>
  <span id="freeText8107618369193446473" style="display:none">'Louboutins, Lattes &amp; Live TV' by Miriam Sawan, is the epitome of guilty pleasure reading. There is plenty of back-stabbing, heaps of drama, and a bucket load of salacious gossip. This talented author has created a novel that is so well-written, and so readable that I finished it in a single day. T is such a page turner - I just had to know what would happen next<br /><br />The story follows Anna-Simone, delighted to land a job at Sky High, a prestigious television network. However, it doesn't take long for the bubble to burst, when her boss Klarissa reveals herself to be ultimate mean girl, a real demon in Louboutins. Klarrissa makes a dream job an absolute nightmare for most of the producers on staff, but Anna-Simone is determined to stand up to her, no matter what it takes. She worked hard for this opportunity and she is not going to let it go without a fight.<br /><br />A real inspiration of a novel, that is the best way to pass the time on a rainy, winter weekend....or to take to the beach on a summer holiday. I highly recommended.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8107618369193446473" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('DNGpdvau2yLZmTHrj+cLWMEtc90bh167NfihD+T9dxQXlvqlSaMlXqXm8NcWXDcP6qp3ZDwJKVQxt7B2N+p8UQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4suqK6R1wKw1G/4l//t/zEuepwEweyZzGcnR454RXQ/5jPn4G3g+0ElkPxlmQEObYBmjuBf1UZwdhsCaTQZWSg==')})
  }

With a foreword by Dame Helen Mirren—the first foreword she has ever contributed.\n\nIn this striking compilation, Shakespeare historian Gerit Quealy and respected Japanese artist Sumié Hasegawa combine their knowledge and skill in this first and only book that examines every plant that appears in the works of Shakespeare.\n\nBotanical Shakespeare opens with a brief look at the Bard’s relationship to the plants mentioned in his works—a diversity that illuminates his knowledge of the science of botany, as well as the colloquy, revealing his unmatched skill for creating metaphorical connections and interweaving substantive philosophy. At the heart of the book are &quot;portraits&quot; of the over 170 flowers, fruits, grains, grasses, trees, herbs, seeds and vegetables that Shakespeare mentions in his plays and poems. Botanical Shakespeare features a gorgeous color illustration of each, giving a &quot;face&quot; to the name, alongside the specific text in which it appears and the character(s) who utter the lines in which it is mentioned.\n\nThis fascinating visual compendium also includes a dictionary describing each plant—such as Eglantine, a wild rose with a slight prickle, cherished for its singular scent, superior to any other rose; and the difference between apples and apple-john—along with indices listing the botanical by play/poem, by character, and genus for easy reference, ideal for gardeners and thoughtful birthday gift-giving.\n\nThis breathtaking, incomparable collection of exquisite artwork and companion quotes offers unique depth and insight into Shakespeare and his timeless work through       <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/17331189.Miriam_Sawan">About Miriam Sawan</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/17331189.Miriam_Sawan"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1510873695p3/17331189.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/17331189.Miriam_Sawan">Miriam Sawan
</a></div>
<div class='goodreadsAuthorBadge'></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
7
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer13564635790377219897">Miriam Sawan is a former television producer turned media advisor who has worked for some of Australia’s biggest television networks. <br/><br/>As a journalist, she always wanted her stories to mean something, and found purpose when she moved to a law firm that works on high profile social justice issues. In her new role as media advisor, she was suddenly exposed to many horrific accounts of workplace bully</span>
  <span id="freeText13564635790377219897" style="display:none">Miriam Sawan is a former television producer turned media advisor who has worked for some of Australia’s biggest television networks. <br /><br />As a journalist, she always wanted her stories to mean something, and found purpose when she moved to a law firm that works on high profile social justice issues. In her new role as media advisor, she was suddenly exposed to many horrific accounts of workplace bullying and was fuelled to write a novel that will resonate with people's office experiences globally. <br /><br />While she can’t tell client stories, writing Louboutins, Lattes &amp; Live TV is her way to “empower young people in the workplace to stand up for themselves and nip nastiness in the bud.”<br /><br /> As for any bullies who read her book, she hopes they’ll learn “to reflect and change old behaviours to stop themselves from the inevitable hurt they cause.” <br /><br />Miriam plans to write for the forseeable future. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13564635790377219897" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
